When booking, I asked for a high floor, wide view, and quiet room type in the notes. The hotel was able to help guests reserve it in advance, which is worthy of recognition. When staying at the hotel, the luxurious decoration that combines Chinese and Western styles is impressive.
During the check-in process, the hotel facilities were unsatisfactory. The bedside control facilities instantly brought people into the 1990s. The plastic texture was cheap and seemed to be incompatible with this intelligent era. Was it to save costs during the decoration? The room was equipped with only one box of paper towels in the bathroom. There was no paper towel for guests to use in the master bedroom, and there was no trash can next to the toilet. The bathroom did not have a dry and wet separation setting, the decoration was simple, and there was no environmentally friendly paper bag in the wardrobe, which was beyond my expectation. When leaving the hotel, the doorman seemed to be a decoration and did not help the guests open the car door.
In short, the hotel‚Äôs service awareness, awareness of details, and service staff‚Äôs speech skills have not yet reached the five-star standard. Advantages:
Jinan Shangri-La has a good geographical location. The facilities are the same as other Shangri-Las, a little old, but the maintenance is OK; the doorman and concierge are enthusiastic, diligent, and the service is good.
Disadvantages:
1. The service concept of the front desk is backward: axis! Poor service awareness! Bringing children to stay for three nights during the holiday, I made a note when booking: I hope to get a higher floor and a room with a better view, but was directly rejected; I asked again at the front desk and was told that I had to pay more, but in any other Shangri-La, the room will be upgraded to members according to the room status (there are rooms that can be upgraded for these three nights); it gives people the feeling that the bad ones are sold first, and the good ones are kept, even if they are empty.
2. The toothbrush in the room is very bad, and it will break your mouth if you are not careful; the bath towels are too old, rough and yellow, and it hurts to wipe the body.
3. Breakfast is worse than other Shangri-La hotels. It is open until 10:30 on holidays, but there is basically nothing left or no additions at 10 o'clock (the Chinese kitchen is okay and is always busy), but the Western kitchen has very few varieties, and even cheese is not served. I told the waiter, but he replied that it was out. I told the front desk, and the waiter said he would get it, but in the end, the food was not served. I asked her and she turned her face away. The second and third days were the same. Finally, I talked to the supervisor, and only a few thin slices were cut, and they were sp****ly placed on a greasy black plate, which felt very dirty; the bread was the same. If you go later, there are basically empty baskets and no additions.
The breakfast room waiter is good, constantly cleaning and collecting plates.
Suggestions:
Shangri-La is an old five-star hotel, and its facilities and equipment are not as good as those of the new five-star hotel, but I always feel that the service is considerate and warm, and customer experience is the first priority. It wins in service and management. Customers are basically old customers, and it is also sentimental;
So Jinan store needs to work harder.

I only know Baotu Spring and Daming Lake with limited culture, so I locked the hotel unit between the two scenic spots. After comparing before and after, I still chose Shangri-La. After all, when I don‚Äôt know anything, the word "Shangri-La" can still be used as the final guarantee. On the way to Jinan, I received a call from Ms. Geng Wenqi, the hotel's customer relationship manager, who asked about the check-in needs very intimately, and added WeChat after obtaining consent, so as to provide better services.
       The location of the hotel is very good, it takes 10-15 minutes to walk to these two attractions. The lobby is still magnificent, and the doorman offered to help push the luggage. Mr. Gao Yigang, who helped me check in, saw that I had two children and took the initiative to upgrade the room type for me, and thoughtfully helped me avoid the breakfast fee for the two children. Putting money aside, this move has improved our check-in experience a lot. Hotel parking is also free, and there is a large ba*****t.
       The hotel's rooms have maintained Shangri-La's usual standards, and a full set of toiletries for children has been specially prepared for children. However, it may be because the positioning of Shangri-La in Haitang Bay, Sanya is slightly different. Shangri-La in Jinan is more business-oriented, while Shangri-La in Sanya is purely casual. The floor-to-ceiling windows are facing Quancheng Square. Due to the high floor, you can have a panoramic view of Baotu Spring and Daming Lake. The fifth floor of the hotel is a swimming fitness spa, and hotel guests can use the swimming pool and gym for free. There are not many people and the water quality is very clean. The locker room has hot and cold water pools, a sauna, and a Finnish bath. Although they are young, they are all clean.
       Did not go out to eat that night. The buffet at the hotel's Cafe Spring Restaurant is a few dollars cheaper for in-house guests than buying coupons on Dianping. On Tuesdays, women can also get a few dollars cheaper. Compared with specialized cafeterias such as Jingcai, Sixth Season, and Mingmen Feast, the variety of dishes is definitely less, but after all, it is a five-star hotel, and the standard it should have is still online. For details, you can refer to Dianping. Good reviews section.
       Apart from the five-star standard of service, environment, facilities, and sanitation, the hotel is located in a busy city and is very convenient in every way. Come to Jinan next time. I think I will choose Shangri-La without hesitation.

Service: It should be said that Jinan Shangri-La basically upholds the concept of "hospitality and hospitality" of the hotel group. From the moment the doorman takes the luggage from his hands, almost every service staff can stop and greet with a smile. The service of the Horizon Club on the fourth floor is as always attentive and thoughtful. From pillows to meal delivery to Band-Aid needs, room service was responsive on several occasions. The active turndown service is also worthy of praise.
Environment: Although the indoor facilities of Jinan Shangri-La feel old, they are just right, not dilapidated and useless. What is still fresh in my memory is the fully automatic electric kettle with a sense of age.
Hygiene: Generally speaking, the hygiene is good and relatively clean. Of course, this may also be because I am not very picky.
Location: Adjacent to the famous scenic spots Baotu Spring and Black Tiger Spring, and not far from Daming Lake, living on a high floor (I live on the 18th floor) can even overlook Daming Lake, which is considered a lake view room. The hotel is facing Jinan's landmark Quancheng Square, and is also facing Ginza, Hang Lung, Guihe shopping malls. While shopping is convenient, the night view at night is also very characteristic of Jinan. But it is estimated that the distance is too close, and the music of the square dance at night can be faintly heard. If you are very sensitive to sound, you need to consider carefully.
Breakfast: Because I don't like crowds and like to have freshly prepared food for breakfast, I am used to dining in the Horizon Club. There are not many varieties, but the a la carte food is fresh and hot. This is a matter of opinion.
Finally, a little regret. Every time I stay in Shangri-La, I have the habit of pulling ****s in the "Shang Palace" restaurant, and experience the exquisite food with local characteristics in each "Shang Palace". So it is a pity to know that there is no Shang Palace restaurant in Jinan Shangri-La at the beginning of the stay.
